func getStringValue(b []rune) (int, error) {
	if b[0] != '"' {
		return 0, NewParseError("strings must start with '\"'")
	}

	endQuote := false
	i := 1

	for ; i < len(b) && !endQuote; i++ {
		if escaped := isEscaped(b[:i], b[i]); b[i] == '"' && !escaped {
			endQuote = true
			break
		} else if escaped {
			/*c, err := getEscapedByte(b[i])
			if err != nil {
				return 0, err
			}

			b[i-1] = c
			b = append(b[:i], b[i+1:]...)
			i--*/

			continue
		}
	}

	if !endQuote {
		return 0, NewParseError("missing '\"' in string value")
	}

	return i + 1, nil
}

func getStringValue(b []rune) (int, error) {
	if b[0] != '"' {
		return 0, NewParseError("strings must start with '\"'")
	}

	endQuote := false
	i := 1

	for ; i < len(b) && !endQuote; i++ {
		if escaped := isEscaped(b[:i], b[i]); b[i] == '"' && !escaped {
			endQuote = true
			break
		} else if escaped {
			/*c, err := getEscapedByte(b[i])
			if err != nil {
				return 0, err
			}

			b[i-1] = c
			b = append(b[:i], b[i+1:]...)
			i--*/

			continue
		}
	}

	if !endQuote {
		return 0, NewParseError("missing '\"' in string value")
	}

	return i + 1, nil
}

	if b[0] != '"' {
		return 0, NewParseError("strings must start with '\"'")
	}

	endQuote := false
	i := 1

	for ; i < len(b) && !endQuote; i++ {
		if escaped := isEscaped(b[:i], b[i]); b[i] == '"' && !escaped {
			endQuote = true
			break
		} else if escaped {

			}

			i--*/

			continue
		}
	}

	if !endQuote {
		return 0, NewParseError("missing '\"' in string value")
	}

	return i + 1, nil
}

### Example 1:
Input:
func getStringValue(b []rune) (int, error) {
	if b[0] != '"' {
		return 0, NewParseError("strings must start with '\"'")
	}

	endQuote := false
	i := 1

	for ; i < len(b) && !endQuote; i++ {
		if escaped := isEscaped(b[:i], b[i]); b[i] == '"' && !escaped {
			endQuote = true
			break
		} else if escaped {
			/*c, err := getEscapedByte(b[i])
			if err != nil {
				return 0, err
			}

			b[i-1] = c
			b = append(b[:i], b[i+1:]...)
			i--*/

			continue
		}
	}

	if !endQuote {
		return 0, NewParseError("missing '\"' in string value")
	}

	return i + 1, nil
}

### Example 1:
Input:
func getStringValue(b []rune) (int, error) {
	if b[0] != '"' {
		return 0, NewParseError("strings must start with '\"'")
	}

	endQuote := false
	i := 1

	for ; i < len(b) && !endQuote; i++ {
		if escaped := isEscaped(b[:i], b[i]); b[i] == '"' && !escaped {
			endQuote = true
			break
		} else if escaped {
			/*c, err := getEscapedByte(b[i])
			if err != nil {
				return 0, err
			}

			b[i-1] = c
			b = append(b[:i], b[i+1:]...)
			i--*/

			continue
		}
	}

	if !endQuote {
		return 0, NewParseError("missing '\"' in string value")
	}

	return i + 1, nil
}

func getStringValue(b []rune) (int, error) {
	if b[0] != '"' {
		return 0, NewParseError("strings must start with '\"'")
	}

	endQuote := false
	i := 1

	for ; i < len(b) && !endQuote; i++ {
		if escaped := isEscaped(b[:i], b[i]); b[i] == '"' && !escaped {
			endQuote = true
			break
		} else if escaped {
			/*c, err := getEscapedByte(b[i])
			if err != nil {
				return 0, err
			}

			b[i-1] = c
			b = append(b[:i], b[i+1:]...)
			i--*/

			continue
		}
	}

	if !endQuote {
		return 0, NewParseError("missing '\"' in string value")
	}

	return i + 1, nil
}

func getStringValue(b []rune) (int, error) {
	if b[0] != '"' {
		return 0, NewParseError("strings must start with '\"'")
	}

	endQuote := false
	i := 1

	for ; i < len(b) && !endQuote; i++ {
		if escaped := isEscaped(b[:i], b[i]); b[i] == '"' && !escaped {
			endQuote = true
			break
		} else if escaped {
			/*c, err := getEscapedByte(b[i])
			if err != nil {
				return 0, err
			}

			b[i-1] = c
			b = append(b[:i], b[i+1:]...)
			i--*/

			continue
		}
	}

	if !endQuote {
		return 0, NewParseError("missing '\"' in string value")
	}

	return i + 1, nil
}
